 Farrukh, who is expert in creating every character as a part of his personality, is not recognized by his talent, with a very simple, effortless and efficient acting
 nasiruddin shah, om puri jaise samanaantar cinema ke kalakaaron ke samaan hi saamanaantar cinema main apane sahaj abhinay kii chhap chhodane ke baavjood unhen vah mukaam naseeb nahin hua, jo unke daur ke anya kalakaaron ko mila
 Farooq also decorated many TV serials in the late 90s with his best performances, including 'miracle' on Sony channel, 'zee Ministerji' on Star plus
farrukh also worked in enditivi dwaara banaae gaye kaarykram 'jeena isi kaa naam he' main bhi farrukh ne kaam kiya
 He also played the lead role in the Doordarshan serial 'srikanth' based on the famous novel by Sharat Chandra Chattopadhyay
 apni sah-abhinetriyon main dipti naval ke saath unki jodi sabase zyada safal rahi
 The pair of Deepti Naval and Farukh Sheikh were the biggest hits of the seventies
 darshak in donon hi behad saral, sahaj dikhne vaale or behad swaabhaavik abhinay karne vaale kalakaaron main khud apni chhavi dekhte the or unhen saath dekhnaa chaahate the
 Together this hit duo did many films like 'chashme Baddoor', 'rang-birangi', 'saath Saath Saath', 'katha' which were also very successful
 ek antaraal ke baad 'saas, bahu or sensex', 'lahore' or 'club 60' jaisi shandaar filmon ke jariye unhone phir se filmon main apni pari kii shuruyaat kii
 In 'lisan Amaya' he reappeared after 25 years with Deepti Naval
 'lahore' main unke shashakt abhinay ke liye unhen sarvshereshth sahaayak abhinayta ke liye rashtriya puraskaar se nawaja gaya
 The comments dil kaa daura padane ke kaaran 2013 main vah duniya ko alavida kar chale gaye, vah bhi apni dharti se nahin, pardes se
 But his fans will always live in the image of him as an actor who may not have been a superstar, but in terms of acting, a star was quite high

 Unable to find his own identity in advocacy, Farrukh then chose acting as a career
 unhone apane kariyar kii shuruyaat theatre se kii
 He worked with the Bharatiya Jan Natya Sangh (IPTA) and well-known director Sagar Sarhadi
 unhen apane samakaleen abhinaytaon ke samaan superstar kaa darja bhale hi na mila ho, lekin apni mehnat, lagan or jeevant abhinay kshamta ke balboote vah sheeghra hi filmi duniya main apni ek alag chhap chhodane main kaamyaab rahe

 gurni ke 'lav letters' par aadhaarit is naatak main farrukh or shabana ko manch par saath dekhnaa darshakon ke liye ek sukhad anubhuti tha
 The play was staged 300 times successfully
 vah ek aise paripurna kalakaar the, jo abhinay ke har manch or chote-bade har kirdaar ko puri vafadari se nibhaate the
 Farukh was also an actor in male dominated films who had no hesitation in playing a small role in Umrao Jaan centered on actress Rekha
 film ke poster par hi nahin, balki puri film main bhi rekha hi chai thim
 But Farrukh did full justice to his role and left the indelible mark of his character of Nawab Sultan
 isi tarah saal 1973 main 'garam hawa' main farrukh shaikh ne sahaayak bhoomika nibhaai thi
 But despite not having a lead role in the film, he managed to leave a strong impression of his strong acting
 sattar ke dashak main jab bollywood main hinsa va maar-dhaad se bharpoor filmon kaa ek nayaa daur shuru ho rahaa tha or bollywood amitabh bachchan kii 'engri yang main' kii chhavi garh rahaa tha, usee samay farrukh apane sahaj abhinay se sine duniya main apni ek alag pahchaan bana rahe the
 He kept the characters of parallel films like 'katha', 'umrao Jaan', 'saath Saath' and 'gaman' alive on screen
 vah ek aise abhinayta kii chhavi gadhane main kaamyaab rahe, jo behad jatil kirdaaron ko bhi behad sahajata se nibhaane or unhen parde par asal jindagi ke kareeb or vaastavik dikhaane main maahir the
 Farrukh worked with noted directors such as Satyajit Ray, Muzaffar Ali, Hrishikesh Mukherjee, Ketan Mehta and Sai Paranjpe
 'gaman' main ek taxi diver ke rup main jeevika kii talash main uttar pradesh se mumbai jane vaala ek hataash or kunthit pravasi yuvak, 'chashme baddoor' main ek sidhaa-sada or sharmila noujvaan va 'katha' main ek chaalaak or dhoort yuvak vasudev va umrao jaan ke jahin nawab, farrukh kaa nibhaayaa har kirdaar vividh prakaar kii bhoomikaaon ko behad khilandadpan or sahajata se bakhubi nibhaane kii unki kshamta ko pramanit karata he
 Theater, poetry, social work, writing, reading, cooking and feeding were many aspects of his personality and his generosity and loyalty towards every aspect was evident
 apane laajawab abhinay se darshakon ko mantrmugdh karne vaale farrukh shaikh ne filmon kii sankhya kii jagah unki gunvattta par dhyaan diya or yahi kaaran he ki apane chaar dashak ke sine kariyar main unhone lagbhag 40 filmon main hi kaam kiya

 farrukh ne film ke saath-saath tivi or theatre main bhi kaam kiya
 Despite being active in films, he was also associated with theater
 shabana azmi ke saath unka naatak 'tumhaari amrutha' behad safal rahaa
 a
 aar
 In this drama based on Gurney's 'love Letters', watching Farrukh and Shabana together on stage was a pleasant feeling for the audience
 is naatak kaa 300 baar safal manchan hua
 He was such a perfect performer who played every stage of acting and every character, big and small, with complete loyalty
 purush pradhan filmon ke daur main bhi farrukh aise abhinayta the, jinhen abhinetri rekha par kendrit umrao jaan main ek chota sa kirdaar nibhaane main bhi koi hichkichaahat nahin thi
 Rekha was not only on the film's poster, but also in the entire film
 lekin farrukh ne apni bhoomika ke saath puraa nyaay kiya or nawab sultan ke apane kirdaar kii amit chhap chhod di
 Similarly in the year 1973, Farooq Sheikh played a supporting role in 'garam Hawa'
 lekin film main mukhya bhoomika na hote hue bhi vah apane damdaar abhinay kii shashakt chhap chhodane main kaamyaab rahe
 In the seventies, when a new era of violence and violence was beginning in Bollywood and Bollywood was creating the image of Amitabh Bachchan's 'angry Young Man', at the same time, Farooq with his spontaneous acting in the cine world Were creating a different identity
 vah 'katha', 'umrao jaan', 'saath-saath' or 'gaman' jaisi samanaantar filmon ke kirdaaron ko parde par jeevant karte rahe
 He managed to create an image of an actor who was very adept at playing even the most complex characters very easily and making them appear closer and real to real life on screen
 farrukh ne satyajit re, mujffar ali, rishikesh mukherjee, kethan mehta or sain paranjape jaise prakhyat nirdeshkon ke saath kaam kiya
 a desperate and frustrated migrant youth from Uttar Pradesh to Mumbai in search of livelihood as a taxi diver in 'gaman', a straightforward and shy young man in 'chashme Baddoor' and a clever and sly young man in 'katha' And each character played by Farooq, the zealous Nawab of Umrao Jaan, testifies to his ability to perform a variety of roles with great finesse and ease
 theatre, shaayari, soshal work, likhnaa-padhanaa, khaanaa pakaana or khilaanaa unke vyaktitv ke kai pahalu the or har pahalu ke prati unki sanjidagi or vafadari dikhti thi
 Farrukh Sheikh, who mesmerized the audience with his brilliant acting, noted his quality rather than the number of films and that is why he worked in only 40 films in his four-decade cine career
 nirmaataa-nirdeshak yash chopra kii film 'nuri' se unhone vyavsaayik filmon main bhi apni abhinay kshamta ko siddh kiya
 Adorned with excellent song and music, the success of this film established not only him but also actress Poonam Dhillon as a star
 behad saadagi bhare, sahaj or kushal abhinay se har kirdaar ko apane vyaktitv ke ek hisse ke rup main gadhane main maahir farrukh ko apni pratibha ke anuroop pahchaan nahin mili
 Despite leaving a mark of his spontaneous performance in the contemporary cinema, similar to actors in parallel cinema like Naseeruddin Shah, Om Puri, he did not get the chance that other actors of his era had
 farrukh ne 90 ke dashak ke ant main kai tivi dharawahikon ko bhi apane behtareen abhinay se sajaayaa, jinamein soni channel par 'chamatkaar', star plus par 'ji mantriji' aadi shaamil the
 Farooq also acted in the program 'jeena Isi Ka Naam Hai' made by NDTV
 unhone sharat chandra chattopadhyaay ke vikhyath upanyaas par aadhaarit doordarshan dharawahik 'shrikant' main bhi mukhya bhoomika nibhaai
 Her pairing with Deepti Naval was the most successful among her co-actresses
 dipti naval or farrukh shaikh kii jodi sattar ke dashak kii sabase hit jodi rahi
 The audience saw their own image in these two very simple, comfortable looking and very natural acting actors and wanted to see them together
 is hit jodi ne saath milakar 'chashme baddoor', 'rang-birangi', 'saath-saath', 'katha' jaisi kai filmein kin, jo behad safal bhi raheen
 After a hiatus, he again made his debut in films with brilliant films like 'saas, Bahu Aur Sensex', 'lahore' and 'club 60'
 'lison amaaya' main vah dipti naval ke saath 25 saal baad phir se dikhaai die
 He won the National Award for Best Supporting Actor for his strong performance in 'lahore'
 tippaniyan He left the world goodbye in 2013 due to a heart attack, not from his own land, but from Pardes

 dipti naval or farrukh shaikh kii jodi sattar ke dashak kii sabase hit jodi rahi
 The audience saw their own image in these two very simple, comfortable looking and very natural acting actors and wanted to see them together
 is hit jodi ne saath milakar 'chashme baddoor', 'rang-birangi', 'saath-saath', 'katha' jaisi kai filmein kin, jo behad safal bhi raheen
 After a hiatus, he again made his debut in films with brilliant films like 'saas, Bahu Aur Sensex', 'lahore' and 'club 60'
 'lison amaaya' main vah dipti naval ke saath 25 saal baad phir se dikhaai die
 He won the National Award for Best Supporting Actor for his strong performance in 'lahore'
 tippaniyan He left the world goodbye in 2013 due to a heart attack, not from his own land, but from Pardes
 lekin unke prashansakon ke jehan main unki chhavi ek aise abhinayta ke rup main sadaiv jivit rahegi, jo superstar bhale hi na rahaa ho, lekin abhinay ke maamle main ek star shakhsiyat se kaaphi oonche mukaam par rahaa
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Similarly in the year 1973, Farooq Sheikh played a supporting role in 'garam Hawa'
 lekin film main mukhya bhoomika na hote hue bhi vah apane damdaar abhinay kii shashakt chhap chhodane main kaamyaab rahe
 In the seventies, when a new era of violence and violence was beginning in Bollywood and Bollywood was creating the image of Amitabh Bachchan's 'angry Young Man', at the same time, Farooq with his spontaneous acting in the cine world Were creating a different identity
 vah 'katha', 'umrao jaan', 'saath-saath' or 'gaman' jaisi samanaantar filmon ke kirdaaron ko parde par jeevant karte rahe
 He managed to create an image of an actor who was very adept at playing even the most complex characters very easily and making them appear closer and real to real life on screen
 farrukh ne satyajit re, mujffar ali, rishikesh mukherjee, kethan mehta or sain paranjape jaise prakhyat nirdeshkon ke saath kaam kiya
 a desperate and frustrated migrant youth from Uttar Pradesh to Mumbai in search of livelihood as a taxi diver in 'gaman', a straightforward and shy young man in 'chashme Baddoor' and a clever and sly young man in 'katha' And each character played by Farooq, the zealous Nawab of Umrao Jaan, testifies to his ability to perform a variety of roles with great finesse and ease
 theatre, shaayari, soshal work, likhnaa-padhanaa, khaanaa pakaana or khilaanaa unke vyaktitv ke kai pahalu the or har pahalu ke prati unki sanjidagi or vafadari dikhti thi
 Farrukh Sheikh, who mesmerized the audience with his brilliant acting, noted his quality rather than the number of films and that is why he worked in only 40 films in his four-decade cine career
 nirmaataa-nirdeshak yash chopra kii film 'nuri' se unhone vyavsaayik filmon main bhi apni abhinay kshamta ko siddh kiya
 Adorned with excellent song and music, the success of this film established not only him but also actress Poonam Dhillon as a star
 behad saadagi bhare, sahaj or kushal abhinay se har kirdaar ko apane vyaktitv ke ek hisse ke rup main gadhane main maahir farrukh ko apni pratibha ke anuroop pahchaan nahin mili
 Despite leaving a mark of his spontaneous performance in the contemporary cinema, similar to actors in parallel cinema like Naseeruddin Shah, Om Puri, he did not get the chance that other actors of his era had
 farrukh ne 90 ke dashak ke ant main kai tivi dharawahikon ko bhi apane behtareen abhinay se sajaayaa, jinamein soni channel par 'chamatkaar', star plus par 'ji mantriji' aadi shaamil the
 Farooq also acted in the program 'jeena Isi Ka Naam Hai' made by NDTV

 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Theater, poetry, social work, writing, reading, cooking and feeding were many aspects of his personality and his generosity and loyalty towards every aspect was evident
 apane laajawab abhinay se darshakon ko mantrmugdh karne vaale farrukh shaikh ne filmon kii sankhya kii jagah unki gunvattta par dhyaan diya or yahi kaaran he ki apane chaar dashak ke sine kariyar main unhone lagbhag 40 filmon main hi kaam kiya
 With producer-director Yash Chopra's film 'noori', he also proved his acting ability in commercial films
 behtareen geet-sangeet or abhinay se saji is film kii kamyaabi ne na sirf unhen, balki abhinetri punam dhillon ko bhi star ke rup main sthapit kar diya
 Farrukh, who is expert in creating every character as a part of his personality, is not recognized by his talent, with a very simple, effortless and efficient acting
 nasiruddin shah, om puri jaise samanaantar cinema ke kalakaaron ke samaan hi saamanaantar cinema main apane sahaj abhinay kii chhap chhodane ke baavjood unhen vah mukaam naseeb nahin hua, jo unke daur ke anya kalakaaron ko mila
 Farooq also decorated many TV serials in the late 90s with his best performances, including 'miracle' on Sony channel, 'zee Ministerji' on Star Plus
 enditivi dwaara banaae gaye kaarykram 'jeena isi kaa naam he' main bhi farrukh ne kaam kiya
 He also played the lead role in the Doordarshan serial 'srikanth' based on the famous novel by Sharat Chandra Chattopadhyay
 apni sah-abhinetriyon main dipti naval ke saath unki jodi sabase zyada safal rahi
 The pair of Deepti Naval and Farukh Sheikh were the biggest hits of the seventies
 darshak in donon hi behad saral, sahaj dikhne vaale or behad swaabhaavik abhinay karne vaale kalakaaron main khud apni chhavi dekhte the or unhen saath dekhnaa chaahate the
 Together this hit duo did many films like 'chashme Baddoor', 'rang-birangi', 'saath Saath Saath', 'katha' which were also very successful
 ek antaraal ke baad 'saas, bahu or sensex', 'lahore' or 'club 60' jaisi shandaar filmon ke jariye unhone phir se filmon main apni pari kii shuruyaat kii
 In 'lisan Amaya' he reappeared after 25 years with Deepti Naval
 'lahore' main unke shashakt abhinay ke liye unhen sarvshereshth sahaayak abhinayta ke liye rashtriya puraskaar se nawaja gaya
 The comments dil kaa daura padane ke kaaran 2013 main vah duniya ko alavida kar chale gaye, vah bhi apni dharti se nahin, pardes se
 But his fans will always live in the image of him as an actor who may not have been a superstar, but in terms of acting, a star was quite high

 shaayad hi cricket ke itihaas main pehle kabhi aisa hua ho jab camentator kii baton par gaur karte hue field main maujuud captain ne gendbaaji main parivartan kiya ho
 The commentators as well as the captain are also being criticized after the incident
 australia cricket board ne bhi is par apni naaraazgi jataai he
 The comments bataa den, buudhvaar ko sidney thunder or edilade strikers ke bich hue match ke dauraan aisa hua
 Batting first, the strikers scored a total of 178 runs at the loss of five wickets in the prescribed 20 overs
 vahiin, jeet ke lakshya kaa peechha karte hue sidney thunder kii taraf se shen watson salaami ballebaaji ke rup main maidan par maujuud the
 While the fourth over was underway, commentator Mark Howard, sitting in the commentary box, told Strikers captain Brad Hodge on talkback that strikers bowler Ben Laughlin had dismissed Shane Watson twice in the last eight balls and Hodge replied that In the next over he would call Laughlin to bowl

 lekin duusari pari main kiwi ballebaaj nahin chale or puri team mahaj 220 ranon par dher ho gai

 cricket kaa makka kahe jane vaale lords par 1884 se lekar ab tak kul 130 test match khele ja chuke hai lekin yah keval teesraa aisa avasar he jab yahaan ek match main 1,600 se adhik ran bane hai
 The record for the highest score in a match on this ground was 1,603 runs, which was made in the Test match played between England and India in 1990
 australia or england ke bich 1930 main khele gayi match main is maidan par 1,601 ran bane the

 yahaan unka siti scan or baaki test kiye gaye
